The <abbr> element in HTML is used to mark abbreviations and acronyms, offering a semantic indication that a sequence of characters represents a shortened form of a longer word or phrase. The element supports the title attribute, which provides the full version of the abbreviation, enhancing accessibility by allowing screen readers and browsers to display or vocalize the expanded meaning. 

The <abbr> element does not visually alter the text by default, but it allows styling via CSS and improves machine readability, indexing, and assistive technology performance. ^efm8wl68
